  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=4.8)
    The plot lacks a clear arc and feels more like a character study without meaningful progression. The connection between cooking experiments and dueling remains abstract rather than concrete. While there's a conceptual beginning (finding the chest) and end (closing it with renewed hope), the middle lacks substantive development or conflict. The story tells us transformation is happening without showing the process through specific events or challenges.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=6.4)

The resolution feels somewhat rushed and too easily achieved given the presumed difficulty of charming a fearsome monster.
